```python
# We'll now remove side symbols and instead fill left/right sides with shaded boxes using a golden-ratio gradient
# We'll still keep the central line as `4ll m0ments` (with no space within each word)
# and center it in a 48-character-wide panel using gradient shading blocks on both sides

# Redefine poem core
poem_core = "4ll m0ments"
panel_width = 48

# Define gradient of shaded blocks (5 steps)
shading_gradient = ['‚ñë', '‚ñí', '‚ñì', '‚ñà', '‚ñ†']

# Calculate left/right padding size
total_padding = panel_width - len(poem_core)
half_padding = total_padding // 2

# Distribute gradient left to right based on golden-style weighting
def make_shade_bars(length, shades):
    block_size = max(1, length // len(shades))
    blocks = []
    for i, s in enumerate(shades):
        blocks.extend([s] * block_size)
    # pad if necessary
    if len(blocks) < length:
        blocks.extend([shades[-1]] * (length - len(blocks)))
    return "".join(blocks[:length])

left_shade = make_shade_bars(half_padding, shading_gradient)
right_shade = make_shade_bars(half_padding, list(reversed(shading_gradient)))

# Compose the centered line
centered_line = f"{left_shade}{poem_core}{right_shade}"

# Build full block with 2 top, 5 middle, 2 bottom rows
top_shade = shading_gradient[-1] * panel_width
bottom_shade = shading_gradient[-2] * panel_width
scroll_block = [top_shade, top_shade] + [centered_line] * 5 + [bottom_shade, bottom_shade]

"\n".join(scroll_block)
```

## Prompt:
Analyzed

```python
# Now we apply the same centered logic to lines 2 and 3
# Each line will:
# - Use its own elemental gradient (FIRE and WATER)
# - Display the line centered with golden-ratio shading on sides
# - Below the line: generate a column-wise field where each unique letter appears in an equal number of columns
#   using different field shapes: rain (line 1), spiral-like (line 2), grid/network (line 3)

from collections import Counter
import random

def build_centered_panel(poem_core, panel_width, element_gradient, symbol_field_type):
    total_padding = panel_width - len(poem_core)
    half_padding = total_padding // 2

    # Side shading
    left_shade = make_shade_bars(half_padding, element_gradient)
    right_shade = make_shade_bars(half_padding, list(reversed(element_gradient)))
    centered_line = f"{left_shade}{poem_core}{right_shade}"
    centered_line = centered_line[:panel_width].ljust(panel_width)

    # Top and bottom elemental borders
    top_border = element_gradient[-1] * panel_width
    bottom_border = element_gradient[-2] * panel_width

    # Repeat central poem line
    poem_lines = [centered_line] * 5

    # Generate glyph field underneath
    unique_letters = list(set(poem_core.replace(" ", "")))
    columns = list(range(panel_width))
    random.shuffle(columns)

    letter_cycle = unique_letters * ((panel_width // len(unique_letters)) + 1)
    assigned_letters = dict(zip(columns, letter_cycle))

    field_rows = []

    # FIELD TYPES
    for row_idx in range(5):
        row = ""
        for col in range(panel_width):
            if symbol_field_type == "rain":
                # Straight down
                row += assigned_letters.get(col, '¬∑')
            elif symbol_field_type == "spiral":
                # Spiral‚Äîalternate direction by row
                if row_idx % 2 == 0:
                    row += assigned_letters.get(col, '¬∑')
                else:
                    rev_col = panel_width - col - 1
                    row += assigned_letters.get(rev_col, '¬∑')
            elif symbol_field_type == "network":
                # Grid pattern
                char = assigned_letters.get(col, '¬∑')
                row += char if (row_idx + col) % 2 == 0 else '¬∑'
        field_rows.append(row)

    return [top_border, top_border] + poem_lines + [bottom_border, bottom_border] + field_rows

# Define poem cores and gradients
panel_width = 48
poems = [
    {
        "text": "4ll m0ments",
        "gradient": ['‚ñë', '‚ñí', '‚ñì', '‚ñà', '‚ñ†'],  # AIR
        "field": "rain"
    },
    {
        "text": "l0ST TIM3",
        "gradient": ['.', ':', '+', '#', '‚éØ'],  # FIRE
        "field": "spiral"
    },
    {
        "text": "TE4R(S) R4IN",
        "gradient": ['‚ê£', ':', '=', '‚ñì', '‚ñà'],  # WATER
        "field": "network"
    }
]

# Build each panel
scroll_panels = []
for p in poems:
    panel = build_centered_panel(p["text"], panel_width, p["gradient"], p["field"])
    scroll_panels.append(panel)

# Combine all into a final scroll
full_scroll = "\n\n".join(["\n".join(panel) for panel in scroll_panels])
full_scroll
```

```python
import random

# Add 5 more rows beneath each panel for a total of 10 after-columns
# Options in each column: either a shading char (1‚Äì10), a blank space, or a unique poem character

# Extended shading characters from light to dark (10 levels)
shade_chars_10 = [' ', '.', ':', '-', '=', '+', '*', '#', '‚ñì', '‚ñà']

# Retrieve unique characters from all poem lines
all_poem_text = ["4ll m0ments", "l0ST TIM3", "TE4R(S) R4IN"]
unique_chars = set("".join("".join(all_poem_text).split()))
unique_chars = list(unique_chars)

# Function to generate extended field
def generate_field_block(panel_width, num_rows, fill_options):
    field_rows = []
    for _ in range(num_rows):
        row = ""
        for _ in range(panel_width):
            row += random.choice(fill_options)
        field_rows.append(row)
    return field_rows

# Apply for each of the three panels
scroll_panels_extended = []
for p in poems:
    base_panel = build_centered_panel(
        poem_core=p["text"],
        panel_width=panel_width,
        element_gradient=p["gradient"],
        symbol_field_type=p["field"]
    )
    # Append 5 more rows with new fill logic
    fill_options = shade_chars_10 + [' '] + unique_chars
    extra_rows = generate_field_block(panel_width, 5, fill_options)
    scroll_panels_extended.append(base_panel + extra_rows)

# Merge into one full scroll output
extended_scroll = "\n\n".join(["\n".join(panel) for panel in scroll_panels_extended])
extended_scroll
```

Analyzed

```python
# Reconstruct the triptych scroll with perfect symmetry and gutters.
# Each panel is 48 characters wide, and we insert 5 gutter columns between them.
# Ensure alignment of all lines and consistent structure across all 3 panels.

# Constants
panel_width = 48
gutter_width = 5
total_panels = 3

# Function to wrap a single panel into a full layout line
def wrap_panels(panel_a, panel_b, panel_c, gutter='     '):
    max_height = max(len(panel_a), len(panel_b), len(panel_c))
    full_layout = []
    for i in range(max_height):
        a_line = panel_a[i] if i < len(panel_a) else ' ' * panel_width
        b_line = panel_b[i] if i < len(panel_b) else ' ' * panel_width
        c_line = panel_c[i] if i < len(panel_c) else ' ' * panel_width
        full_layout.append(f"{a_line}{gutter}{b_line}{gutter}{c_line}")
    return full_layout

# Use previous final panels already generated
panel1 = scroll_panels_extended[0]
panel2 = scroll_panels_extended[1]
panel3 = scroll_panels_extended[2]

# Wrap into final layout
symmetrical_triptych_scroll = wrap_panels(panel1, panel2, panel3)

# Save final scroll
with open("/mnt/data/te4rs_r4in_triptych_FINAL_SCROLL_vŒ©_RECTIFIED.txt", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write("\n".join(symmetrical_triptych_scroll))

"/mnt/data/te4rs_r4in_triptych_FINAL_SCROLL_vŒ©_RECTIFIED.txt"
```

```python
# Rebuild the scroll using exact structure:
# - 3 vertical panels (I, II, III)
# - Each panel has:
#   - 5 header lines
#   - 20 body lines
#   - Total = 25 lines per panel (to be scaled up by golden ratio if needed)
# Gutter columns will be 5 spaces wide
# Panel width = 48

from math import ceil

# Helper to generate dummy panel content for demonstration
def make_panel_block(text, gradient, width, header_height=5, body_height=20):
    header_block = [gradient[-1] * width for _ in range(header_height)]
    body_line = text.center(width, gradient[2])
    body_block = [body_line for _ in range(body_height)]
    return header_block + body_block

# Define gradients for each panel
air_gradient = ['‚ñë', '‚ñí', '‚ñì', '‚ñà', '‚ñ†']     # Panel I
fire_gradient = ['.', ':', '+', '#', '‚éØ']   # Panel II
water_gradient = ['‚ê£', ':', '=', '‚ñì', '‚ñà']  # Panel III

# Panel poem lines
panel_texts = ["4ll m0ments", "l0ST TIM3", "TE4R(S) R4IN"]

# Build panels
panel1_block = make_panel_block(panel_texts[0], air_gradient, panel_width)
panel2_block = make_panel_block(panel_texts[1], fire_gradient, panel_width)
panel3_block = make_panel_block(panel_texts[2], water_gradient, panel_width)

# Wrap with 5-space gutter between panels
triptych_layout = wrap_panels(panel1_block, panel2_block, panel3_block)

# Calculate golden ratio extensions (e.g. 1.618 * base height)
golden_rows = ceil(len(triptych_layout) * 1.618)
padded_layout = triptych_layout + [' ' * (panel_width * 3 + 10)] * (golden_rows - len(triptych_layout))

# Save to file
final_path = "/mnt/data/te4rs_r4in_triptych_FINAL_SCROLL_vŒ©_GOLDEN.txt"
with open(final_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    f.write("\n".join(padded_layout))

final_path
```
